		trigger = {
			804 = {
				check_variable = { TUR_arab_state_level > 0 }
				TUR_is_controlled_by_us_or_subject_vilayet = yes
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_arab_population_stability_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_stability_factor = 0 } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_war_support_factor = 0 } }
					}
					AND = {
						has_variable = TUR_arab_population_political_power_factor
						NOT = { check_variable = { TUR_arab_population_political_power_factor = 0 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
